across multiple components:\\n\\n## 1. User Authentication Implementation\\n\\n**File**: `arangod/Auth/User.h` and `arangod/Auth/User.cpp`\\n**Key Class**: `User`\\n\\nThe `User` class represents a user entry and stores access levels for databases and collections. Key methods include:\\n- `checkPassword()` - Verifies user password against stored hash\\n- `checkAccessToken()` - Validates access tokens\\n- `grantDatabase()` and `grantCollection()` - Grant access rights\\n- `databaseAuthLevel()` and `collectionAuthLevel()` - Resolve access levels\\n\\n## 2. User Management System\\n\\n**Files**: \\n- `arangod/Auth/UserManager.h` - Abstract interface\\n- `arangod/Auth/UserManagerImpl.h` and `arangod/Auth/UserManagerImpl.cpp` - Concrete implementation\\n\\n**Key Classes**: `UserManager` (abstract) and `UserManagerImpl` (implementation)\\n\\nThe UserManager is the sole point of access for user and permission management stored in `_system/_users`. It provides:\\n- User CRUD operations\\n- Credential validation via `checkCredentials()` method\\n- Access level resolution for databases and collections\\n- User caching with periodic updates from database\\n- Access token management\\n\\n## 3. JWT Token Validation for REST API\\n\\n**Files**: `arangod/Auth/TokenCache.h` and `arangod/Auth/TokenCache.cpp`\\n**Key Class**: `TokenCache`\\n\\nThe TokenCache implements JWT token validation with the following key methods:\\n- `checkAuthentication()` - Main authentication entry point\\n- `checkAuthenticationBasic()` - HTTP Basic authentication validation\\n- `checkAuthenticationJWT()` - JWT token validation\\n- `validateJwtHeader()` - Validates JWT header format\\n- `validateJwtBody()` - Extracts and validates JWT payload\\n- `validateJwtHMAC256Signature()` - HMAC SHA256 signature validation\\n- `validateJwtES256Signature()` - EC ES256 signature validation\\n- `Entry` - Inner class representing cached authentication results with expiry tracking\\n\\n## 4. Authorization Context (Permission Checking)\\n\\n**File**: `arangod/Utils/ExecContext.h`\\n**Key Class**: `ExecContext`\\n\\nThe ExecContext class carries execution context information and enforces authorization for database operations:\\n- `canUseDatabase()` - Checks if user has sufficient permission level for a database\\n- `canUseCollection()` - Checks if user has permission for a collection\\n- `databaseAuthLevel()` - Returns user's permission level on current database\\n- `collectionAuthLevel()` - Returns user's permission level on specific collection\\n- `isAdminUser()` - Indicates if user has admin privileges\\n- `isSuperuser()` - Indicates if context is superuser (internal operations)\\n- Thread-local `CURRENT` - Maintains current execution context\\n\\n## 5. User Management REST Endpoint\\n\\n**Files**: `arangod/RestHandler/RestUsersHandler.h` and `arangod/RestHandler/RestUsersHandler.cpp`\\n**Key Class**: `RestUsersHandler`\\n\\nImplements the `/_api/user` REST endpoint for user management:\\n- `getRequest()` - List users\\n- `postRequest()` - Create user\\n- `putRequest()` - Update user\\n- `patchRequest()` - Partial user update\\n- `deleteRequest()` - Delete user\\n- `generateUserResult()` - Format user response\\n\\n## 6. Authentication REST Endpoints\\n\\n**Files**: \\n- `arangod/RestHandler/RestAuthHandler.h` and `.cpp` - Main authentication endpoint\\n- `arangod/RestHandler/RestAccessTokenHandler.h` and `.cpp` - Access token management endpoint\\n- `arangod/RestHandler/RestAuthReloadHandler.h` and `.cpp` - Authentication reload endpoint\\n\\n**Key Classes**: `RestAuthHandler`, `RestAccessTokenHandler`, `RestAuthReloadHandler`\\n\\nThese handlers manage authentication:\\n- `RestAuthHandler::generateJwt()` - Generates JWT tokens for authenticated users\\n- `RestAccessTokenHandler` - Manages user access tokens for programmatic access\\n- `RestAuthReloadHandler` - Reloads authentication configuration\\n\\n## 7. Authentication Configuration and Settings\\n\\n**Files**:\\n- `arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationFeature.h` and `.cpp` - Main authentication feature\\n- `arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationOptions.h` - Configuration options\\n\\n**Key Class**: `AuthenticationFeature`\\n\\nThe AuthenticationFeature manages authentication initialization and configuration:\\n- `collectOptions()` - Registers command-line options including:\\n  - `--server.authentication` - Enable/disable authentication (default: true)\\n  - `--server.authentication-timeout` - Session timeout (default: 0.0)\\n  - `--server.authentication-system-only` - Limit to system database (default: true)\\n  - `--server.authentication-unix-sockets` - Auth for Unix sockets (default: true)\\n  - `--server.jwt-secret` - Inline JWT secret\\n  - `--server.jwt-secret-keyfile` - JWT secret from file\\n  - `--server.jwt-secret-folder` - JWT secrets from folder\\n- `loadJwtSecretsFromFile()` - Loads JWT secrets from configured sources\\n- `loadJwtSecretKeyfile()` - Loads JWT secret from keyfile\\n- `loadJwtSecretFolder()` - Loads JWT secrets from folder\\n\\nDefault authentication settings in `AuthenticationOptions`:\\n- `authenticationUnixSockets = true`\\n- `authenticationSystemOnly = true`\\n- `active = true`\\n- `sessionTimeout = 3600.0` (1 hour)\\n- `minimalJwtExpiryTime = 10.0` (10 seconds)\\n- `maximalJwtExpiryTime = 3600.0` (3600 seconds)\\n\\n## 8. Authorization Levels\\n\\n**File**: `arangod/Auth/Common.h`\\n**Key Enum**: `Level`\\n\\nDefines permission levels:\\n- `UNDEFINED = 0` - No access level defined\\n- `NONE = 1` - No access\\n- `RO = 2` - Read-only access\\n- `RW = 3` - Read-write access\\n\\n## 9. HTTP Communication Authentication\\n\\n**Files**: `arangod/GeneralServer/CommTask.h` and `.cpp`\\n\\nThe CommTask classes handle HTTP request processing including authentication:\\n- Validates authentication headers from HTTP requests\\n- Checks if user is authenticated before processing requests\\n- Maintains authentication state throughout request processing\\n\\n## 10. Handler Interface\\n\\n**File**: `arangod/Auth/Handler.h`\\n**Key Classes**: `Handler`, `HandlerResult`\\n\\nDefines pluggable authentication handler interface for potential RBAC systems:\\n- `Handler::authenticate()` - Authenticates user and returns permissions/roles\\n- `Handler::readPermissions()` - Reads user permissions assuming prior authentication\\n- `HandlerResult` - Encapsulates authentication results with role information\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe ArangoDB authentication and authorization infrastructure is built on:\\n1. **User model** (`User` class) with password and token validation\\n2. **User management** (`UserManager` interface with `UserManagerImpl` implementation)\\n3. **JWT validation** (`TokenCache` with support for HMAC256 and ES256)\\n4. **Permission enforcement** (`ExecContext` for operation-level authorization)\\n5. **REST endpoints** for user and authentication management\\n6. **Configurable feature** (`AuthenticationFeature`) with JWT secret management\\n7. **HTTP-level integration** via `CommTask` for request authentication\\n\\nAll authentication happens at multiple levels: HTTP request processing, REST handler processing, and database operation execution through ExecContext permission checks.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
